 ########## USER INPUT ##########

 USER INPUT FILE

 #
 # general
 #
 projectile p
 element ni
 mass 62
 energy 1.012195122 15.18292683 1.012195122e-1
 #
 #select level density
 ldmodel 1
 outdensity y
 filedensity y
 #
 #select strength
 strength 1
 strengthm1 3
 outgamma y
 filepsf y
 #
 # accuracy cutoffs
 xseps 1.e-20
 transeps 1.e-20
 transpower 15
 popeps 1.e-20
 #
 # increase number of bins and use equidistant spacing
 bins 80
 equidistant y
 #
 # switch preequilibrium off
 preequilibrium no
